#—Å–≤–µ–∫—Ä–æ–≤—å/—Ç—ë—â–∞ –≤ –∑–∞–≤–∏—Å–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –æ—Ç –ø–æ–ª–∞ –∏–≥—Ä–æ–∫–∞ (–≤—ã–∑—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ [Player.])
defined_text = {
	name = GetMotherInLaw

	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { character = FROM }
			is_female = yes
		}
		localisation_key = GetRelation_MotherOfHusband
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { character = FROM }
			is_female = no
		}
		localisation_key = GetRelation_MotherOfWife
	}
	fallback_text = {
		localisation_key = GetMotherInLaw_FB
	}
}

	name = GetConcubineWife

	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { character = FROM }
			is_female = no
			NOT = { is_senior_consort_party = yes }

		}
		localisation_key = GetConcubineWife_Wife
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { character = FROM }
			is_female = no
			is_senior_consort_party = yes
		}
		localisation_key = GetConcubineWife_Concubine
	}
	fallback_text = {
		localisation_key = GetConcubineWife_FB
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name =  #GetHalfSiblingAdj

	text = {
		trigger = {
			#multiplayer = no
			NOT = { character = FROM }
			#mother_even_if_dead = { any_child_even_if_dead = { ai = no } }
			mother_even_if_dead = { any_child_even_if_dead = { character = ROOT } }
		}
		localisation_key = String_MothersChildAdj
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			#multiplayer = no
			NOT = { character = FROM }
			#father_even_if_dead = { any_child_even_if_dead = { ai = no } }
			father_even_if_dead = { any_child_even_if_dead = { character = ROOT } }
		}
		localisation_key = String_FathersChildAdj
	}
}

			}

		}
		localisation_key = END_AYA_
	}
	text = {

		localisation_key = REL_FRIEND_MALE_CAP
	}
}
